<script type="text/javascript">vpn_eval((function(){

    function autoExpand(tid) {
        var node = facetComponent.facetTree.getNodeByTId(tid);
        if (node.children[10].isHidden) { //被隐藏的状态
            $("#SS" + tid).html("更少&nbsp;<<");
            facetComponent.facetTree.showNodes(node.children);
        }
        else {
            $("#SS" + tid).html("更多&nbsp;>>");
            for (var i = 10; i < node.children.length; i++) {
                facetComponent.facetTree.hideNode(node.children[i]);
            }
        }
    }

    function Facet() {
        this.FacetRequest = [];
        this.facetTree = null;
        this.facetResults = null;
        //删除聚类条件
        this.removeFacet = function (that) {
            var data = Enumerable.from(this.FacetRequest).firstOrDefault("$.id==" + resultComponent.ActiveId);
            data.fields.splice($(that).parent().index(), 1);
            $(that).parent().remove()
            facetComponent.refreshSearching();
        };

        //获取当前筛选的聚类条件
        this.getFacetRequestVo = function () {
            var ret = []
            $.each($(".list-group-item"), function (index, element) {
                ret.push({
                    field: $(element).attr("datafield"),
                    query: $(element).attr("dataquery"),
                    name: $(element).attr("dataname"),
                    facetname: $(element).attr("facetname"),
                    id: $(element).attr("dataid"),
                    level: $(element).attr("datalevel")
                });
            });
            return ret;
        };

        this.beforeClick = function (treeId, treeNode) {
            if (treeNode.level == 0) {
                var zTree = $.fn.zTree.getZTreeObj("facetTree");
                zTree.expandNode(treeNode);
                return false;
            }
            return true;
        };

        this.refreshSearching = function () {
            facetComponent.isFacetSearch = true;
            doSearching(0, resultComponent.ActiveId);
        };

        //聚类点击事件响应
        this.onFacetClick = function (event, treeId, treeNode) {
            var pnode = treeNode.getParentNode();
            //加入新的facet条件，需要保存到分类对象
            var rq = {
                facetname: pnode.name,
                field: pnode.field,
                query: treeNode.query,
                level: pnode.level,
                id: treeNode.id,
                name: treeNode.name
            };
            facetComponent.addFacetRequest(rq);
            if (treeNode.name) {
                facetComponent.refreshSearching();
            }
        };

        this.addFacetRequest = function (rq) {
            var data = Enumerable.from(facetComponent.FacetRequest).firstOrDefault("$.id==" + resultComponent.ActiveId);
            if (data) {
                data.fields.push(rq);
            }
            else {
                facetComponent.FacetRequest.push({id: resultComponent.ActiveId, fields: [rq]});
            }
            $("#facetConditions").append(Handlebars.templates.facetrequest(rq));
        };

        this.addDiyDom = function (treeId, treeNode) {
            var spaceWidth = 5;
            var switchObj = $("#" + treeNode.tId + "_switch"),
                icoObj = $("#" + treeNode.tId + "_ico"),
                textObj = $("#" + treeNode.tId + "_span");
            switchObj.remove();
            icoObj.before(switchObj);
            if (treeNode.level > 1) {
                var spaceStr = "<span style='display: inline-block;width:" + (spaceWidth * treeNode.level) + "px'></span>";
                switchObj.before(spaceStr);
            }
            if (treeNode.level == 1 && !treeNode.children) {
                var badge = "<span class='badge'>" + treeNode.count + "</span>";
                textObj.parent().after(badge);
            }
            if (treeNode.level == 0 && treeNode.children.length > 10) {
                textObj.parent().after("<span style='cursor:pointer;' id='SS" + treeNode.tId + "' onclick='autoExpand(\"" + treeNode.tId + "\");'>" +
                    "更多&nbsp;>></span>");
            }
        };

        //聚类树显示
        this.setting = {
            view: {
                addDiyDom: this.addDiyDom,
                showLine: false,
                showIcon: false,
                dblClickExpand: false,
                selectedMulti: false
            },
            callback: {
                beforeClick: this.beforeClick,
                onClick: this.onFacetClick
            }
        };

        //显示学科树
        this.showSubjectClassTree = function (subjectclass) {
            if (subjectclass == null || subjectclass.length == 0) {
                $("#divSc").addClass("invisible");
            }
            else {
                $("#divSc").removeClass("invisible");
            }
            var addMydom = function (treeId, treeNode) {
                var textObj = $("#" + treeNode.tId + "_span");
                var badge = "<span class='badge'>" + treeNode.count + "</span>";
                textObj.parent().addClass("w75");
                textObj.parent().after(badge);
            };

            var ptsetting = {
                view: {
                    addDiyDom: addMydom,
                    showIcon: true,
                    dblClickExpand: false,
                    selectedMulti: false
                },
                data: {
                    key: {
                        name: "name",
                        children: "children"
                    }
                },
                callback: {
                    onClick: this.onSubjectClassClick
                }
            };

            var treeObj = $("#scTree");
            $.fn.zTree.init(treeObj, ptsetting, subjectclass);
        };

        //学科分类树点击
        this.onSubjectClassClick = function (event, treeId, treeNode) {
            bksy.post("/literature/scstastic", {scid: treeNode.id, type: 0});
            //加入新的facet条件，需要保存到分类对象
            var rq = {
                facetname: "学科分类",
                field: "CLC",
                query: "",
                level: 1,
                id: treeNode.id,
                name: treeNode.name
            };
            facetComponent.addFacetRequest(rq);
            if (treeNode.name) {
                facetComponent.refreshSearching();
            }
        };

        //显示聚类项目
        this.showFacets = function (facetresults) {

            this.facetResults = facetresults;
            for (var j = 0; j < facetresults.length; j++) {
                var ele = facetresults[j];
                if (ele.children != null && ele.children.length > 10) {
                    for (var i = 10; i < ele.children.length; i++) {
                        ele.children[i].isHidden = true;
                    }
                }
            }
            console.log(facetresults)
            var treeObj = $("#facetTree");
            this.facetTree = $.fn.zTree.init(treeObj, this.setting, Enumerable.from(facetresults).where("$.field!='Year'").toArray());
            treeObj.addClass("showIcon");
//            treeObj.hover(function () {
//                if (!treeObj.hasClass("showIcon")) {
//                    treeObj.addClass("showIcon");
//                }
//            }, function () {
//                treeObj.removeClass("showIcon");
//            });
            //显示年份聚类
            var years = Enumerable.from(facetresults).firstOrDefault("$.field=='Year'");
            if (years) {
                this.showColumn(years);
            } else {
                $("#yearDiv").addClass("invisible");
                $('#customCharts').children().remove();
            }
            //切换聚类筛选项
            var data = Enumerable.from(this.FacetRequest).firstOrDefault("$.id==" + resultComponent.ActiveId);
            $("#facetConditions").html("");
            if (data) {
                $.each(data.fields, function (index, rq) {
                    $("#facetConditions").append(Handlebars.templates.facetrequest(rq));
                });
            }
        };

        //显示图表
        this.showColumn = function (result) {
            $("#yearDiv").removeClass("invisible");
            $("#yearHeader").html(result.name);
            $('#customCharts').highcharts({
                    chart: {
                        backgroundColor: "",
                        type: 'column',
                        zoomType: "x",
                        events: {

                                //alert(this.xAxis[0].userMin + " : " + this.xAxis[0].userMax);

                        }
                    },
                    title: {
                        text: result.name,
                        floating: true,
                        style: {"visibility": "hidden"}
                    },
                    xAxis: {
                        categories: Enumerable.from(result.children).select("$.name").toArray(),
                        minRange: 0.5
                    },
                    yAxis: {
                        min: 0,
                        endOnTick: false,
                        title: {
                            enabled: false
                        }
                    },
                    legend: {
                        enabled: false
                    },
                    tooltip: {
                        formatter: function () {
                            return '<span style="font-size:10px">' + this.x + '</span>' + '<table><tbody><tr><td style="color:{series.color};padding:0"></td><td style="padding:0"><a href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="facetYear(\'' + this.x + '\')"><b>' + this.points[0].point.extra + '&nbsp;' +
                                '项</b></a></td></tr></tbody></table>';
                        },
                        shared: true,
                        useHTML: true
                    },
                    plotOptions: {
                        column: {
                            borderWidth: 0
                        },
                        series: {
                            cursor: 'pointer',
                            events: {
                                click: function (event) {
                                    facetYear(event.point.category);
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    series: [{
                        name: "十年统计",
                        data: Enumerable.from(result.children).select("{y:$.count,extra:$.displayCount}").toArray()
//                            ,dataLabels: {
//                                enabled: true,

                }

//                //动态更新
//                chart.series[0].update({
//                    pointWidth: columnWidth
//                });
//            }
            );
        };

        //清空聚类项
        this.clearFacets = function () {
            var treeObj = $("#facetTree");
            $.fn.zTree.init(treeObj, this.setting, null);
            $("#divSc").addClass("invisible");
            var sctree = $("#scTree");
            $.fn.zTree.init(sctree, this.setting, null);
            $('#customCharts').children().remove();
            $("#yearDiv").addClass("invisible");
            $("#facetConditions").html("");
            this.FacetRequest = [];
        };
    }

    function facetYear(category) {
        var result = Enumerable.from(facetComponent.facetResults).firstOrDefault("$.field=='Year'");
        var fq = Enumerable.from(result.children).first("$.name=='" + category + "'");
        facetComponent.addFacetRequest({
            facetname: result.name,
            field: result.field,
            query: fq.query,
            level: result.level,
            id: fq.id,
            name: fq.name
        });
        facetComponent.refreshSearching();
    }

    //1秒5次以上弹窗提醒全局变量
    var flag = true;
    var firstClickTime = 0;
    var fiveClickTime = 0;
    var clickCount = 0;

    function confirmBrowseEntity(eid,bc,pid,activeId,source) {

        //1秒5次以上弹窗提醒全局变量
        clickCount++;
        var date = new Date();
        var clickTime = date.getTime();
        if(flag){
            firstClickTime = clickTime;
            flag = false;
        }
        if (clickCount >5){
            fiveClickTime = clickTime;
            flag = true;
            clickCount = 0;
        }
        if(fiveClickTime > firstClickTime){
            var end = fiveClickTime - firstClickTime ;
            if(end < 1000){
                return msgConfirm("点击太快哦，请慢点！")
            }
        }

        bksy.post("/literature/browseEntityAsk", {
            eid: eid
        }, function (sr) {
            console.log(sr)
            if (sr.status == 0) {
                newwindow = window.open();
                if (sr.successMessage != null && sr.successMessage != "") {
                    var url = encodeURIComponent(prepareUrl("/literature/browseEntity/" + eid, ["bc", "pid", "activeId"], [bc, pid, activeId]));
                    $.cookie('msgs', encodeURIComponent(sr.successMessage), {expires: 1, path: '/'});
                    $.cookie('okmsg', encodeURIComponent('确定'), {
                        expires: 1,
                        path: '/'
                    });
                    $.cookie('cancelmsg', encodeURIComponent('取消'), {
                        expires: 1,
                        path: '/'
                    });
                    newwindow.location = '/public/messages/msg.html?url=' + url;
                }
                else {
                    browseEntity(eid, bc, pid, activeId, source);
                }
            }else if (sr.status == -2){
                msgConfirm('<div class="form-group">\n' +
                    '                <label for="verifyCode">验证码：</label>\n' +
                    '                <div class="row">\n' +
                    '                    <div class="col-md-6">\n' +
                    '                        <input type="text" class="form-control" name="verifyCode" id="verifyCode" placeholder="">\n' +
                    '                    </div>\n' +
                    '                    <div class="col-md-6">\n' +
                    '                        <img style="display:inline-block;width: 100%" id="kaptcha" src="/kaptcha.jpg" title=\'点击更换验证码\'\n' +
                    '                             onclick="javascript:refreshCaptcha();"/>\n' +
                    '                    </div>\n' +
                    '                </div>\n' +
                    '            </div>',function (index){
                    var code = $("#verifyCode").val();
                    bksy.post("/literature/checkCode", {code:code}, function (res) {
                        console.log(res)
                        if (res.status == 0){
                            browseEntity(eid, bc, pid, activeId, source);
                        }else{
                            layer.msg(res.msg, {icon: 5, type: 0, shade: false, rate: 'top', shadeClose: true});
                        }
                    });

                })
            }
            else {
                msgError(sr.message)
            }
        });
        return false;
    }

    function confirmBrowsePiece2(pid,ltid,activeId,source) {

        var pdfobject = new PDFObject({url: "sample.pdf"});
        if (!pdfobject.foundPlugin()) {
            if (newwindow!=null){

            msgError("您没有安装任何可以嵌入浏览器进行pdf浏览的工具，请安装Adobe pdf reader或其他pdf工具后再使用此功能！")

        }

            pieceId: pid,
            ltid: ltid,
            source: 1    //预览
        }, function (sr) {

    var flagDownload = true;
    var firstDownloadClickTime = 0;
    var fiveDownloadClickTime = 0;
    var clickDownloadCount = 0;

    function confirmDownload(eid,bc,pid,ltid,activeId,source) {

        //1秒5次以上弹窗提醒全局变量
        clickDownloadCount++;
        var date = new Date();
        var clickTime = date.getTime();
        if(flagDownload){
            firstDownloadClickTime = clickTime;
            flagDownload = false;
        }
        if (clickDownloadCount >5){
            fiveDownloadClickTime = clickTime;
            flagDownload = true;
            clickDownloadCount = 0;
        }
        if(fiveDownloadClickTime > firstDownloadClickTime){
            var end = fiveDownloadClickTime - firstDownloadClickTime ;
            if(end < 1000){
                return msgConfirm("点击太快哦，请慢点！")
            }
        }

        bksy.post("/literature/downloadPieceAsk", {
            eid: eid,
            bcId: bc,

    function browseEntity(eid,bc,pid,activeId,source) {
        if (source == null || source == undefined){
            source = "OTHER";
        }
        newWinUrl("/literature/browseEntity/" + eid, ["bc", "pid","activeId","source"], [bc, pid,activeId, source]);
    }

    function browsePiece(eid,bc,pid,ltid,activeId, downloadSource) {
        if (downloadSource == null || downloadSource == undefined){
            downloadSource = "NONE";
        }
        newWinUrl("/literature/browsePiece", ["eid", "bcId", "pieceId", "ltid", "activeId", "downloadSource"], [eid, bc, pid, ltid, activeId,downloadSource]);
    }

    function downloadPiece(eid,bc,pid,ltid,activeId, downloadSource) {
        if (downloadSource == null || downloadSource == undefined){
            downloadSource = "NONE";
        }
        newWinUrl("/literature/downloadPiece", ["eid", "bcId", "pieceId", "ltid", "activeId","source", "downloadSource"], [eid, bc, pid, ltid, activeId,"2",downloadSource]);
    }

<script type="text/javascript">vpn_eval((function(){

    var show = false;
    function enterPage(event) {
        if (event.keyCode == "13") {
            resultComponent.gotoPage();
        }
    }

    function showBigImage(id) {
        var imgsrc = $("#" + id).prop("src");
        var photoJson = {
            "title": "",
            "id": 123,
            "start": 0,
            "data": [
                {
                    "pid": 666,
                    "src": imgsrc,
                    "thumb": ""
                }
            ]
        };
        layer.photos({
            photos: photoJson
            , anim: 5 //0-6的选择，指定弹出图片动画类型，默认随机（请注意，3.0之前的版本用shift参数）
        });
    }

    function PieceResults() {
        //检索结果集合
        this.SearchResults = [];
        this.TotalCount = 0;
        this.ActiveId = 0;
        //刷新显示结果, 多页呈现
        this.ShowResults = function (results, tab, content) {
            if (results.length == 0) {
                msgError("您目前不具备任何产品检索权限，无法检索数据，请先申请试用或购买产品!");
            }
            this.SearchResults = results;
            results.showType = showType();
            if (tab) {
                $("#" + tab).html(Handlebars.templates.searchTab({data: results}));           //显示TAB的，
            }
            $("#" + content).html(Handlebars.templates.piece({data: results}));//显示内容的
            this.updatePager(results, this);
            this.ActiveId = 0;
            if (this.ActiveId == 0 && results.length > 0) {
                this.ShowPieceType(results[0].typeid);
            }
        };

        this.updatePager = function (results, that) {
            that.TotalCount = 0;
            $.each(that.SearchResults, function (index, element) {
                that.TotalCount += element.totalCount;
            });
            $.each(results, function (index, element) {
                if (element.totalCount > 0) {
                    element.curPage = 1;
                    $("#totalpage" + element.typeid).html(element.pageCount);
                    $("#currentCount" + element.typeid).html("当前显示第1-" + element.documents.length + "&nbsp;条");
                    element.Paging = $("#paging" + element.typeid).paging(element.totalCount, {
                        format: "[ < . nnncnnn > ]",
                        perpage: element.pageSize,
                        page: 1,
                        onSelect: function (page) {
                            if (page != element.curPage) {
                                doSearching(page, element.typeid, false);
                                window.scrollTo(0, 0);
                            }
                        },
                        onFormat: function (type) {
                            switch (type) {
                                case 'block':
                                    if (!this.active)
                                        return '<li class="disabled"><a href="#">' + this.value + '</a></li>';
                                    else if (this.value != this.page)
                                        return '<li><a href="#' + this.value + '">' + this.value + '</a></li>';
                                    return '<li class="active"><a href="#">' + this.value + '</a></li>';
                                case 'next':
                                    if (this.active)
                                        return "<li><a href='#" + this.value + "' class='next'>下页</a></li>";
                                    return "<li class='disabled'><a href='#'>下页</a></li>";
                                case "prev":
                                    if (this.active)
                                        return "<li><a href='#" + this.value + "' class='next'>前页</a></li>";
                                    return "<li class='disabled'><a href='#'>前页</a></li>";
                                case "first":
                                    if (this.active)
                                        return "<li><a href='#" + this.value + "' class='next'>首页</a></li>";
                                    return "<li class='disabled'><a href='#'>首页</a></li>";
                                case "last":
                                    if (this.active)
                                        return "<li><a href='#" + this.value + "' class='next'>末页</a></li>";
                                    return "<li class='disabled'><a href='#'>末页</a></li>";
                                case "leap":
                                    if (this.active)
                                        return "   ";
                                    return "";
                                case 'fill':
                                    if (this.active)
                                        return "<li><a href='javascript:void(0);'>...</a></li>";
                                    return "";
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }
                else {
                    $("#pageex" + this.typeid).hide();
                    $("#paging" + this.typeid).hide();
                }
            });
        };

        this.AddResult = function (result, content) {
            var find = false;
            for (var i = 0; i < this.SearchResults.length; i++) {           //更新一下结果
                if (this.SearchResults[i].typeid == result[0].typeid) {
                    this.SearchResults[i] = result[0];
                    find = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!find) {
                this.SearchResults.push(result[0]);
            }
            $("#rt_" + this.ActiveId).remove();     //删除原来的内容
            result.showType = showType();               //传入显示类型
            $("#" + content).append(
                Handlebars.templates.piece({data: result})
            );
            this.updatePager(result, this);
            if (typeof(facetComponent) != "undefined") {
                facetComponent.showFacets(result[0].facetResults);
                facetComponent.showSubjectClassTree(result[0].subjectClasses)
            }
        };

        this.AddTushuResult = function (result, content) {
            var find = false;
            for (var i = 0; i < this.SearchResults.length; i++) {           //更新一下结果
                if (this.SearchResults[i].typeid == result[0].typeid) {
                    this.SearchResults[i] = result[0];
                    find = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!find) {
                this.SearchResults.push(result[0]);
            }
            $("#rt_" + this.ActiveId).remove();     //删除原来的内容
            $("#" + content).append(
                Handlebars.templates.piece(result[0])
            );
            this.updatePager(result, this);
            if (typeof(facetComponent) != "undefined") {
                facetComponent.showFacets(result[0].facetResults);
                facetComponent.showSubjectClassTree(result[0].subjectClasses)
            }
        };

        this.RefreshCurrent = function () {
            for (var i = 0; i < this.SearchResults.length; i++) {
                if (this.SearchResults[i].typeid == this.ActiveId) {
                    this.RefreshSingleResult([this.SearchResults[i]]);
                    break;
                }
            }
        };

        //单页刷新 , 要分正文、图片、广告
        this.RefreshSingleResult = function (result) {
            $("#rt_" + result[0].typeid + " div.resultRow").remove();   //删除原来的内容
            for (var i = 0; i < this.SearchResults.length; i++) {
                if (this.SearchResults[i].typeid == result[0].typeid) {
                    this.SearchResults[i].activeId = result[0].activeId;
                    this.SearchResults[i].fields = result[0].fields;
                    this.SearchResults[i].curPage = result[0].curPage;
                    this.SearchResults[i].documents = result[0].documents;
                    //this.SearchResults[i].facetResults = result[0].facetResults;
                    this.SearchResults[i].subjectClasses = result[0].subjectClasses;
                    this.SearchResults[i].lastQuery = result[0].lastQuery;
                    this.SearchResults[i].lastPrettyQuery = result[0].lastPrettyQuery;
                    break;
                }
            }
            var sc = ((result[0].curPage - 1) * result[0].pageSize) + 1;
            var ec = sc + result[0].documents.length - 1;
            $("#currentCount" + result[0].typeid).html("当前显示第" + sc + "-" + ec + "&nbsp;条");
            if (result[0].typeid == 1) {
                if (showType() == "0")   //简要信息
                    $("#rt_" + result[0].typeid).prepend(
                        Handlebars.templates.article(result[0])
                    );
                else                //详细信息
                    $("#rt_" + result[0].typeid).prepend(
                        Handlebars.templates.articleDetail(result[0])
                    );
            } else if (result[0].typeid == 2) {
                $("#rt_" + result[0].typeid).prepend(
                    Handlebars.templates.pic(result[0])
                );
            } else {
                $("#rt_" + result[0].typeid).prepend(
                    Handlebars.templates.ad(result[0])
                );
            }
        };

        this.findResult = function (typeid) {
            for (var i = 0; i < this.SearchResults.length; i++) {
                if (this.SearchResults[i].typeid == typeid) {
                    return this.SearchResults[i];
                }
            }
            return null;
        };

        //显示指定文章类型结果
        var exportPieceType = 1;
        this.ShowPieceType = function (typeid, callback) {
            exportPieceType = typeid;
            if (this.ActiveId != typeid) {
                if (typeid != 1) {
                    $(".resultShowType").addClass("invisible");
                }
                else {
                    $(".resultShowType").removeClass("invisible");
                }

                $(".tab a").removeClass("selected");
                $(".srTable").addClass("invisible");        //原来活跃的结果框关闭
                this.ActiveId = typeid;
                $("#tab_" + this.ActiveId).addClass("selected");          //设置新的活跃

        this.gotoPage = function () {
            var re = /^[1-9]+[0-9]*]*$/;
            var pg = $("#gpage" + this.ActiveId).val();
            if (!re.test(pg)) {
                msgError("请输入正整数");
                $("#gpage" + this.ActiveId).focus();
                return;
            }
            var page = parseInt(pg);
            var result = this.findResult(this.ActiveId);
            if (page > result.pageCount) {
                msgError("输入的页面超出范围，请重新输入!");
                $("#gpage" + this.ActiveId).focus();
                return;
            }
            result.Paging.setPage(page);
        };

                        period: "WEEK"
                    }
                })

    var prepareRequest = function (typeid) {
        var start = parseInt($("#startYear_" + typeid).val());
        var end = parseInt($("#endYear_" + typeid).val());
        if (start > end) {
            msgError('起始年份小于结束年份！');
            return null;
        }
        var fields = [];
        var contents = [];
        var combines = [];
        var types = [];
        //处理第一个条件
        $.each($("#sf_" + typeid + " .combineLine"), function (index, ele) {
            var field = $(ele).find("select.searchingField").val();
            var content = $(ele).find("input.advSearch").val();
            var combinetype = $(ele).find("select.combineType").val();
            var searchType = $(ele).find("select.searchType").val();

            if (content) {
                if (combinetype && fields.length > 0) {
                    combines.push(combinetype);
                }
                fields.push(field);
                contents.push(content);
                types.push(searchType);
            }
        });

        return {
            start: start,
            end: end,
            searchType: $("#scbtype_" + typeid).val(),
            fields: fields,
            literatureId: 'ffad8c4aafb1081d058b6f54bfc12c6b',
            contents: contents,
            types: types,

            lastPrettyQuery: $("#pquery_" + typeid).html()
        };
    };

    var doSearching = function (pageId, typeId,restarted) {
        if(restarted==false) {
            restarted = false;
        }
        else {
            restarted = true;
        }

        console.log(params)
        if (!params) {    //检测未通过
            return;
        }

        params.isQueryChange=params.isRestart;
        if(facetComponent && facetComponent.isFacetSearch==true) {
            facetComponent.isFacetSearch = false;
            params.isQueryChange = false;
        }

            pageCount: $("#srPageCount").val(),
            asc: $("#srAsc").val(),
            relative: $("#srRelative").val(),
            typeId: typeId,
            facets: facetComponent.getFacetRequestVo()
        };

        $.extend(params, page);  //扩展一下json对象
        if (pageId) {    //针对单个类型的检索
            $.extend(params, {currentPage: pageId})

                $("#pquery_" + result[0].typeid).html(result[0].lastPrettyQuery);
            }
            rc++;
            $("#queryCount").html(result[0].totalCount);
        });
    };

    function Searching(id) {

<script>vpn_eval((function(){

    Date.prototype.Format = function (fmt) { //author: meizz 
        var o = {
            "M+": this.getMonth() + 1, //月份 
            "d+": this.getDate(), //日 
            "h+": this.getHours(), //小时 
            "m+": this.getMinutes(), //分 
            "s+": this.getSeconds(), //秒 
            "q+": Math.floor((this.getMonth() + 3) / 3), //季度 
            "S": this.getMilliseconds() //毫秒 
        };
        if (/(y+)/.test(fmt)) fmt = fmt.replace(RegExp.$1, (this.getFullYear() + "").substr(4 - RegExp.$1.length));
        for (var k in o)
            if (new RegExp("(" + k + ")").test(fmt)) fmt = fmt.replace(RegExp.$1, (RegExp.$1.length === 1) ? (o[k]) : (("00" + o[k]).substr(("" + o[k]).length)));
        return fmt;
    };

    $(document).ajaxStart(function () {
        setActiveTime();
    });

    var CAT = "ClientActiveTime";

    function setActiveTime() {
        var exp = new Date();
        exp.setTime(exp.getTime() + 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
        document.cookie = CAT + "=" + escape(moment().format("x")) + ";path=/;expires=" + exp.toGMTString();
    }

    //获取Cookie
    function getActiveTime() {
        var arr, reg = new RegExp("(^| )" + CAT + "=([^;]*)(;|$)");
        if (arr = document.cookie.match(reg))
            return moment(parseInt(arr[2])).toDate();
        else
            return null;
    }

    function closeWindow() {
        window.opener = null;
        window.open('', '_self');
        window.close();
    }

    setActiveTime();

    var siteTimeout = 720000;           //毫秒, 12分钟提醒
    //var siteTimeout = 10000;           //毫秒, 12分钟提醒
    var beginDate = new Date();         //起始时间
    var noticeTimeout = function () {
        var timeout = 3 * 60;
        var activetime = getActiveTime();
        if (activetime > beginDate) {         //存在其他页面出现活跃
            beginDate = activetime;
            setTimeout("noticeTimeout()", beginDate.getTime() - (new Date()).getTime() + siteTimeout);
        }
        else {
            var interval = null;
            layer.confirm('您的会话将在&nbsp;<span id="time">180</span>&nbsp;秒后过期...', {
                title: '提示',
                btn: ['继续访问']
            }, function (index) {
                layer.close(index);
                bksy.post("/common/keepAlive", null, function () {
                    if (interval !== null) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                    }
                    setTimeout("noticeTimeout()", siteTimeout);
                });
            }, function (index) {
                layer.close(index);
            });

            interval = setInterval(function () {
                $("#time").html(--timeout);
                if (timeout === 0) {
                    layer.closeAll();
                    var date = new Date();
                    var ds = date.Format("hh:mm:ss");
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    layer.confirm('您的会话已经在&nbsp;' + ds + '&nbsp;过期了，您可以选择离开本网站或继续访问！', {
                        title: '提示',
                        btn: ['重新登录', '退出']
                    }, function (index) {
                        layer.close(index);
                        window.location.reload();
                    }, function (index) {
                        closeWindow();
                    });
                }
            }, 1000);
        }
    };
    setTimeout("noticeTimeout()", siteTimeout);


}
